### [65] [Plainbook: Data Science, in Plain Language](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05717v1)
*Luca de Alfaro,Mathis Aubert,Ranjit Jhala,Eliana Pastor,Elena Baralis*

Main category: cs.HC

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: Plainbook通过以自然语言描述为中心、自动生成代码、线性执行和内置验证机制，使得不熟悉代码的科学家也能使用可重现的计算分析。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Jupyter Notebook需要理解代码才能使用，限制了不熟悉代码但需要数据分析和计算的科学家受众。

Method: Plainbook基于两个原则：提升自然语言描述并验证数值。保留自然语言描述，自动生成代码；采用线性执行语义消除隐藏状态；内置基于数值检查的验证机制（单元测试和全局验证），并由快照内核支持高效执行和验证。

Result: Plainbook使得不熟悉代码的用户能够通过自然语言和验证机制使用可重现计算分析，并保证执行顺序和正确性。

Conclusion: 通过以自然语言为中心的设计和验证机制，Plainbook扩大了可重现计算分析的受众，让更多科学家能参与数据分析与计算。

中文摘要：Jupyter Notebook已在数据科学中被广泛采用，因为它允许共享可重现的计算分析。然而，只有理解计算机代码的人才能使用它们。为了触达对数据分析和计算感兴趣但不熟悉代码的更广泛科学家群体，我们推出了Plainbook——一种以自然语言而非代码为中心的笔记本。Plainbook基于两个原则：提升自然语言描述，并验证数值。在Plainbook中，自然语言描述被保留，而不是生成的代码；代码从单元格描述中自动生成。由于自然语言是从上到下阅读的，Plainbook采用线性执行语义，其中单元格保证按照出现的顺序执行；没有像Jupyter那样的“隐藏状态”或乱序执行。为了让可能不懂代码的用户验证计算的正确性，我们在Plainbook中内置了以数值和数值检查为中心的验证机制。这些机制包括关注单个单元格（类似于单元测试）以及全局机制。线性执行语义和验证机制都基于一个快照内核，该内核缓存执行状态，使执行和验证变得高效。

Original abstract: Jupyter Notebooks have become widely adopted in data science, as they allow the sharing of reproducible computational analysis. They are, however, accessible only to people who understand computer code. To reach the broader audience of scientists interested in data analysis and computation, but unfamiliar with code, we introduce Plainbook, notebooks centered on natural language rather than code.
  Plainbook is based on two principles: promote the natural language descriptions, and verify the values. In plainbook, the natural language descriptions are preserved, rather than the resulting code; the code is generated automatically from the cell descriptions. As natural language is read top to bottom, Plainbook adopts a linear execution semantics, in which cells are guaranteed to be executed in the order in which they appear; there is no "hidden state" or out-of-order execution as in Jupyter. To allow users who may not understand code to verify the correctness of the computation, we have built into Plainbook verification mechanisms centered on values and value inspection. These include mechanisms that focus on individual cells, akin to unit tests, as well as global mechanisms. Both the linear execution semantics, and the verification mechanisms, are underpinned by a snapshot kernel that caches execution states and makes execution and verification efficient.

</details>

### [66] [FORGE: Towards Functional Tool-Use Generalization via Keypoint Trajectory Reasoning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05780v1)
*Chuhao Zhou,Liquan Wang,Shuxin Cao,Xiangyu Chen,Yuxuan Hu,Boyu Ma,Animesh Garg,Jianfei Yang*

Main category: cs.RO

Selection reason: 研究工具使用泛化，方法可启发coding agent工具迁移。

TL;DR: 提出FORGE方法，通过关键点轨迹中间表示将功能推理与动作执行解耦，实现在新工具上的功能泛化，成功率提升2倍以上。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 机器人无法将特定工具的功能泛化到新工具，尽管人类可以；需要弥合感知相似性与动作差异性之间的鸿沟。

Method: 探索中间表示（可供性图像、视频提示、关键点轨迹），发现关键点轨迹最佳；提出FORGE两阶段策略，先预测关键点轨迹，再接地为机器人动作。

Result: 在七工具基准上，FORGE在模拟和现实中均优于SOTA，平均成功率提升2倍以上。

Conclusion: 关键点轨迹是一种有效的中间表示，FORGE实现了功能泛化。

中文摘要：虽然人类可以轻松地重新利用一本书、一块石头或一只鞋来钉钉子，但训练了特定工具的机器人却无法将同样的功能转移到新工具上——我们将这一差距形式化为功能泛化。这些工具共享一个视觉上可识别的共同功能意图，但这种感知上的相似性并不能扩展到动作空间，因为每种工具都需要完全不同的运动模式。为了弥合这一差距，我们探索了中间表示，包括可供性图像、人类视频提示和2D关键点轨迹，发现关键点轨迹在功能表达性和动作可落地性之间取得了最佳平衡。在此基础上，我们提出了功能推理与接地执行（FORGE），这是一个两阶段策略，将功能推理与动作执行解耦：从无动作数据中预测可泛化的关键点轨迹，然后通过有限的演示将其接地到机器人动作中。在一个七工具击打功能基准测试中，FORGE在模拟和现实中均在一系列未见过的工具上持续优于最先进的方法，平均成功率提高了2倍以上。

Original abstract: While humans readily repurpose a book, a stone, or a shoe to drive a nail, robots trained on specific tools fail to transfer the same function to novel ones -- a gap we formalize as functional generalization. Such tools share a common functional intent that is visually recognizable, yet this perceptual similarity does not carry over to action space, where each tool demands an entirely different motor pattern. To bridge this gap, we explore intermediate representations including affordance images, human video prompts, and 2D keypoint trajectories, finding that keypoint trajectories best balance functional expressiveness and action groundability. Building on this, we propose FunctiOnal Reasoning and Grounded Execution (FORGE), a two-stage policy that decouples functional reasoning from action execution: predicting generalizable keypoint trajectories from action-free data, then grounding them into robot actions with limited demonstrations. On a seven-tool hitting-function benchmark, FORGE consistently outperforms state-of-the-art methods on unseen tools in both simulation and the real world, achieving over 2X improvement in average success rate.

</details>

# cs.CL [[Back]](#toc)

### [67] [When Should LLMs Search? Counterfactual Supervision for Search Routing](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05752v1)
*Minho Kim*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 研究何时搜索，涉及agent工具使用决策，可迁移至coding agent检索策略。

TL;DR: 提出实例级搜索路由问题，通过比较无搜索和强制搜索结果构建真值，用监督微调和偏好优化训练路由策略，显著提升路由F1。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 搜索增强语言模型中搜索并非总是有益，需要决定何时搜索以提升任务成功率。

Method: 通过比较无搜索和强制搜索结果构建无搜索/搜索/未解决真值，用监督微调和偏好优化训练路由策略。

Result: Gemma E2B路由宏F1从0.7082升至0.8235，Qwen3.5-4B从0.7053升至0.8365。

Conclusion: 学习策略减少特定模型路由失败，残余未解决案例揭示多源瓶颈。

中文摘要：搜索增强的语言模型可以利用外部证据来弥补参数化知识的局限性，但搜索并非总是有益的：模型可能会对它们已经能够回答的问题发起搜索，或者在更合适的做法是纠正、澄清或放弃时，依赖于有噪声的证据。我们将此问题形式化为一个实例级别的搜索路由问题：决定是否需要搜索来提高相对于无搜索执行的任务成功率。为了获得监督信号，我们比较了同一问题在无搜索和强制搜索下的结果，并基于任务特定的成功构建了一个包含无搜索、搜索和未解决三种状态的真值标签。使用这个真值标签作为评估标准和学习信号，我们通过监督微调和偏好优化来训练搜索路由策略，将Gemma E2B上符合真值条件的示例的路由宏F1从0.7082提高到0.8235，Qwen3.5-4B从0.7053提高到0.8365。进一步的分析表明，学习到的策略减少了特定模型的路由失败：Gemma主要学习了无搜索约束，而Qwen进一步减少了错过的搜索；剩余的未解决案例揭示了涉及模型容量、检索预算、证据使用和策略行为的异构瓶颈。

Original abstract: Search-augmented language models can use external evidence to compensate for limitations in parametric knowledge, but search is not uniformly beneficial: models may call search for questions they can already answer, or rely on noisy evidence when correction, clarification, or abstention would be more appropriate. We formulate this as an instance-level search-routing problem: deciding whether search is needed to improve task success relative to a no-search execution. To derive supervision, we compare no-search and forced-search outcomes for the same question and construct an oracle over NO SEARCH, SEARCH, and UNSOLVED based on task-specific success. Using this oracle as both an evaluation criterion and a learning signal, we train search-routing policies with supervised fine-tuning and preference optimization, improving routing macro-F1 on oracle-eligible examples from 0.7082 to 0.8235 for Gemma E2B and from 0.7053 to 0.8365 for Qwen3.5-4B. Further analysis shows that the learned policies reduce model-specific routing failures: Gemma primarily learns no-search restraint, while Qwen further reduces missed search; residual UNSOLVED cases reveal heterogeneous bottlenecks involving model capacity, retrieval budget, evidence use, and policy behavior.

</details>


### [68] [InfluMatch: Frontier-Quality KOL Search at 4B-Model Cost](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05968v1)
*Krittanon Kaewtawee,Petmongkon Pornpichitsuwan,Natchaya Temyingyong,Nutnicha Laplamoon,Wachiravit Modecrua,Krittin Pachtrachai,Touchapon Kraisingkorn*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: KOL搜索级联系统，使用小模型推理，设计取舍对agent系统有参考价值

TL;DR: 提出一个三阶段级联检索重排推理系统InfluMatch，使用小型开放权重模型在KOL匹配中达到与前沿LLM相当的性能，同时成本大幅降低。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有KOL匹配方法要么忽略语义匹配，要么昂贵且缓慢，需要低成本且高效的方法。

Method: 构建三阶段级联：密集检索→点式重排器评分→推理器逐标准评分，全部使用小型开放权重模型（4B），仅在重排器上使用SimPO成对微调。

Result: 在11个查询集上，P@5达94.1%，匹配前沿模型Kimi-K2.6（91.8%），输出token减少35倍，延迟约20秒/50个KOL。

Conclusion: 通过精心设计的级联和选择性微调，可以用小型模型实现可部署、可解释、低成本的KOL搜索系统，避免直接微调推理器的陷阱。

中文摘要：将影响者（KOL）匹配到泰国自由形式、多部分营销标准，目前要么通过关键词搜索结构化资料（这忽略了语义匹配），要么通过提示前沿LLM检查每个候选人（准确但缓慢且昂贵）。我们提出InfluMatch，一个低成本的三阶段级联——检索→重排→推理——完全由小型开放权重模型构建：密集检索返回50个候选人，一个4B点式重排器通过单个Yes token的对数概率对每个评分并保留10个，一个4B推理器根据带有泰语理由的评分标准对短名单逐标准评分。该级联设计用于成本：在过滤后的前10名上进行推理，将token花费减半，同时得分高出14分。端到端针对具有所有50个候选人标签的11个查询集的人类相关性标签，完整级联达到94.1%的P@5，而仅检索基线接近随机；它与前沿模型Kimi-K2.6（91.8%）匹配，同时输出约35倍的token，并在一个A100上约20秒内处理50个KOL的查询。值得注意的是，唯一有效的微调是成对微调：经过SimPO微调的重排器匹配前沿基线的最佳选择准确率（78.0 EM），而在逐标准标签上微调推理器提高了离线得分但降低了端到端排名——我们将这个反转追溯到绝对标签任务的设计——使得未微调的基础模型成为最强大的部署推理器。结果是一个可部署、可解释的KOL搜索系统，成本仅为前沿服务的一小部分。

Original abstract: Matching influencers (KOLs) to free-form, multi-part Thai marketing criteria is today served either by keyword search over structured profiles, which misses semantic fit, or by prompting frontier LLMs over every candidate, which is accurate but slow and expensive. We present InfluMatch, a low-cost three-stage cascade -- retrieval $\rightarrow$ rerank $\rightarrow$ reason -- built entirely from small open-weight models: dense retrieval returns 50 candidates, a 4B pointwise reranker scores each by the log-probability of a single Yes token and keeps 10, and a 4B reasoner grades the shortlist per criterion on a rubric with a Thai rationale. The cascade is designed for cost: reasoning over a filtered top-10 halves token spend versus reasoning over all 50 while scoring 14 points higher. End-to-end against human relevance labels on an 11-query set with all 50 candidates labeled, the full cascade reaches 94.1% P@5, versus a retrieval-only baseline near random; it matches the frontier model Kimi-K2.6 (91.8%) while emitting ${\sim}35\times$ fewer output tokens and serving a 50-KOL query in ${\sim}20$ s on one A100. Notably, the only fine-tuning that pays off is pairwise: a SimPO-tuned reranker matches the frontier baseline's best-pick accuracy (78.0 EM), whereas fine-tuning the reasoner on pointwise per-criterion labels improves offline scores yet degrades end-to-end ranking -- an inversion we trace to the design of the absolute labeling task -- leaving the untuned base model as the strongest deployed reasoner. The result is a deployable, explainable KOL search system at a small fraction of frontier serving cost.

</details>


### [69] [From Blueprint to Reality: Modeling and Applying Putnam's Social Capital Theory with LLM-based Multi-agent Simulations](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06080v1)
*Shiyi Ling,Zhi Zheng,Hui Zheng,Wenjun Xue,Feng Ye,Tong Xu*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 基于LLM的多agent社会仿真框架，可迁移。

TL;DR: SocaSim是一个基于LLM的多智能体模拟框架，通过社会网络、信任和规范三个维度模拟集体行动，应用于智慧养老，重现宏观模式并实现微观因果路径的追踪。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统实证方法在控制和可复制性上有限制，现有LLM社会模拟缺乏与帕特南社会资本理论一致的环境，因此需要构建理论对齐的模拟框架。

Method: 构建SocaSim框架，整合社会网络演化、信任动态和规范传播，让智能体参与重复集体行动实验，并通过逐轮模拟和反事实干预分析因果路径。

Result: 模拟再现了帕特南的宏观模式，群体层面实现人机对齐，并能追踪社会网络、信任和规范的微观因果路径，提供过程级可解释性。

Conclusion: SocaSim建立了一个利用LLM智能体连接社会科学与计算机科学的研究范式，推动理论模拟与实证分析的结合。

中文摘要：帕特南的社会资本理论是集体行动和社区繁荣的基础框架。然而，传统的实证方法在控制和可复制性方面面临实际限制。与此同时，基于大语言模型(LLM)的社会模拟通常是行为驱动的，缺乏与理论一致的环境来建模帕特南的核心命题。为了解决这些差距，我们引入了SocaSim，一个基于LLM的多智能体模拟框架，从理论蓝图到模拟现实研究帕特南的社会资本理论。具体来说，我们构建了一个整合社会网络演化、信任动态和规范传播的环境，其中智能体参与重复的集体行动实验，然后应用这三个维度分析智慧养老中的适应挑战。我们的模拟再现了帕特南的宏观模式，并在群体层面表现出强烈的人机对齐。与传统方法不同，SocaSim通过逐轮模拟和反事实干预追踪社会网络、信任和规范的微观因果路径，实现了过程级别的可解释性。总之，这些能力建立了一个利用LLM智能体连接社会科学和计算机科学的研究范式。

Original abstract: Putnam's Social Capital Theory is a foundational framework for collective action and community prosperity. However, traditional empirical methods face practical limits on control and replication. Meanwhile, LLM-based social simulations are typically behavior-driven and lack theory-aligned environments for modeling Putnam's core propositions. To address these gaps, we introduce SocaSim, an LLM-based multi-agent simulation framework to study Putnam's Social Capital Theory from theoretical blueprint to simulated reality. Specifically, we build an environment integrating social network evolution, trust dynamics, and norm propagation, where agents engage in repeated collective-action experiments, and then apply the three dimensions to analyze adaptation challenges in smart elderly care. Our simulations reproduce Putnam's macro-level patterns and exhibit strong human-agent alignment at the group level. Unlike traditional methods, SocaSim traces micro-level causal pathways of social network, trust, and norms via round-by-round simulations and counterfactual interventions, enabling process-level interpretability. Taken together, these capabilities establish a research paradigm that leverages LLM agents to bridge social science and computer science.

### [70] [LLM Agents for Deliberative Collaboration: A Study on Joint Decision Making Under Partial Observability](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06157v1)
*Chenxu Wang,Yongkun Yang,Boyuan Du,Shiwei Lin,Huaping Liu*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 研究基于LLM的多agent协作决策，提供benchmark和系统评估，可迁移到coding agent协作场景。

TL;DR: 本文研究了部分可观察联合决策任务中LLM智能体的深思熟虑协作，发现复杂任务仍具挑战性，但深思熟虑过程可提供反思和纠错机会。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 人类协作中深思熟虑至关重要，但LLM智能体在部分可观察环境下的协作能力尚未被充分研究。

Method: 形式化深思熟虑协作问题，构建可扩展基准，设计参考框架和评估协议，对多种LLM进行系统评估。

Result: 复杂深思熟虑协作任务对当前LLM仍有挑战；外部工具帮助有限；深思熟虑过程可提升性能。

Conclusion: 为评估和改进LLM在深思熟虑协作中的能力奠定基础，揭示了当前多智能体系统的优缺点。

中文摘要：在协作中，深思熟虑起着关键作用；当人类共同工作时，他们自然地通过交流来对齐信息并达成一致。在本文中，我们研究了部分可观察联合决策任务下的深思熟虑大型语言模型（LLM）智能体。我们将深思熟虑协作形式化为具有部分和非对称观察的协作联合决策问题，并引入了一个可扩展的基准，该基准在多个任务设置和领域中实例化此问题，其中智能体必须通过深思熟虑交换信息以达成具有共享奖励的联合决策。然后，我们实例化了一个用于深思熟虑智能体的参考框架和评估协议，并对一系列代表性LLM进行了系统评估。结果表明，复杂的深思熟虑协作任务仍然对最先进的语言模型构成挑战。即使在外部数学工具的帮助下，语言模型可能在信息对齐的深思熟虑过程或做出决策的复杂推理过程中失败。另一方面，诊断分析揭示，深思熟虑过程也可能提供反思和错误纠正的机会，有时能提高性能优于集中式基线。总之，我们的工作为评估和改进深思熟虑协作中的LLM智能体奠定了基础，并提供了对当前基于LLM的多智能体系统的优势、局限性和特性的见解。

Original abstract: Deliberation plays a crucial role in collaboration; when humans work together, they naturally engage in communication to align information and reach an agreement. In this paper, we investigate deliberative large language model (LLM) agents under partially observable joint decision-making tasks. We formalize deliberative collaboration as a cooperative joint decision problem with partial and asymmetric observations, and introduce a scalable benchmark that instantiates this problem across multiple task settings and domains in which agents must exchange information through deliberation to reach a joint decision with a shared reward. We then instantiate a reference scaffold and evaluation protocol for deliberative agents and conduct a systematic evaluation of a range of representative LLMs. The results reveal that complex deliberative collaboration tasks continue to challenge state-of-the-art language models. Even with the aid of external mathematical tools, language models may fail in either the deliberation process for aligning information or the complex reasoning process for making the decision. On the other hand, diagnostic analysis reveals that the deliberation process may also provide opportunities for reflection and error correction, sometimes improving performance over centralized baselines. Altogether, our work establishes a foundation for evaluating and improving LLM agents in deliberative collaboration and provides insights into the strengths, limitations, and properties of current LLM-based multi-agent systems.

</details>


### [71] [Improving LLM-Generated Process Model Quality Through Reinforcement Learning: The Role of Reward Function Design](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06175v1)
*Alexander Rombach,Chantale Lauer,Nijat Mehdiyev*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 利用RL优化LLM生成结构化输出，reward函数设计方法可迁移到agent自我改进。

TL;DR: 通过系统研究奖励函数设计，发现强化学习可显著提升流程模型生成的句法和实用质量，等权奖励优于针对性权重，且设计选择与模型架构存在复杂交互。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的监督微调方法将LLM输出质量限制在训练数据模式内，而强化学习虽可超越这一上限，但多维度质量场景下的奖励函数设计尚未被探索。

Method: 采用组序列策略优化（GSPO）训练Llama 3.1 8B和Qwen 2.5 14B模型，在48种配置下使用包含38个指标（句法、实用、语义）的自动评估框架推导奖励，系统比较不同奖励权重和设计选择。

Result: RL使输出变异性降低六倍以上，并显著提升实用和句法质量；等权奖励始终优于针对性权重；无效惩罚和SFT初始化的效果因模型架构而异。

Conclusion: 奖励组合是优化结果的主要决定因素，其影响与是否应用RL本身一样大，且发现可推广到其他多维度质量评估的结构化生成任务。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）能够从自然语言描述生成BPMN流程模型，然而监督微调（SFT）将其输出质量限制在训练数据中存在的模式。强化学习（RL）可以使用外部质量度量优化超越这一上限，但当质量是多维度时，奖励函数应如何设计仍未被探索。我们提出了一项关于基于RL的流程模型生成的奖励函数设计的系统研究，在48种配置下使用组序列策略优化训练了两个LLM家族（Llama~3.1 8B，Qwen~2.5 14B），奖励来自一个包含38个指标（涵盖句法、实用和语义质量）的自动评估框架。出现了三个发现。首先，RL在保持语义保真度的同时显著提高了实用和句法质量，输出变异性降低了六倍以上。第二，等权奖励始终优于目标权重：强调特定维度不仅未能改进该维度，反而可能使模型崩溃到低质量模式。第三，设计选择与模型架构以非平凡方式交互：无效惩罚对一个模型至关重要，但对另一个模型无关紧要；SFT初始化对一个架构不可或缺，但对另一个架构适得其反。这些结果表明奖励组合是优化结果的主要决定因素，其影响与是否应用RL本身一样大。这些发现可推广到任何通过多个自动维度评估质量的结构化生成任务。我们在https://github.com/chlauer99/RL_for_process_modeling发布了我们的实现和实验代码。

Original abstract: Large language models (LLMs) can generate BPMN process models from natural-language descriptions, yet supervised fine-tuning (SFT) limits their output quality to the patterns present in the training data. Reinforcement learning (RL) can optimize beyond this ceiling using external quality measures, but how the reward function should be designed when quality is multi-dimensional remains unexplored. We present a systematic investigation of reward function design for RL-based process model generation, training two LLM families (Llama~3.1 8B, Qwen~2.5 14B) under 48 configurations using Group Sequence Policy Optimization with rewards derived from an automated evaluation framework comprising 38 metrics across syntactic, pragmatic, and semantic quality. Three findings emerge. First, RL significantly improves pragmatic and syntactic quality while preserving semantic fidelity, reducing output variability by more than sixfold. Second, equal reward weighting consistently outperforms targeted weighting: emphasizing a specific dimension fails to improve it and can collapse the model into a low-quality mode. Third, design choices interact with model architecture in non-trivial ways: the invalidity penalty is essential for one model but irrelevant for the other, and SFT initialization is indispensable for one architecture but counterproductive for another. These results demonstrate that reward composition is a primary determinant of optimization outcomes, with effects as large as the decision to apply RL itself. The findings generalize to any structured generation task where quality is assessed along multiple automated dimensions. We release our implementation and experimental code at https://github.com/chlauer99/RL_for_process_modeling.

</details>


### [72] [Spider 2.0-AIFunc: Extending Real-World Text-to-SQL to AI-Native SQL Workflows](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06229v1)
*Tianyang Liu,Canwen Xu,Fangyu Lei,Nikki Lijing Kuang,Jixuan Chen,Tao Yu,Julian McAuley,Zhewei Yao,Yuxiong He*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 扩展text-to-SQL benchmark至AI原生SQL，评估agent框架在软件工程任务上的表现。

TL;DR: 提出了Spider 2.0-AIFunc基准，用于评估AI原生SQL生成，发现最强专有模型准确率67-70%，开源模型58.1%，且传统Agent框架效果不佳。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有文本到SQL基准不支持AI原生SQL，需要新的基准来评估模型在AI原生SQL上的生成能力。

Method: 基于现有企业文本到SQL基准，通过Agent流水线将源任务重写为AI原生形式，构建465个验证实例，覆盖六种AI函数，并采用多轮重复执行协议确保结果稳定性。

Result: 最强专有模型执行准确率67-70%，最佳开源模型58.1%，错误主要集中在谓词规范、模式基础和AI函数参数化上。

Conclusion: 传统Agent框架在AI原生SQL上无效，简单Agent设置即可达到或超越复杂方案的效果。

中文摘要：大型云数据平台现在将大语言模型能力作为原生SQL函数暴露，使分析师能够在普通SQL查询中执行分类、过滤、情感分析、提取、相似性搜索和聚合等操作。然而，现有的文本到SQL基准仅评估传统SQL，无法判断模型是否能生成这种AI原生SQL。我们提出了Spider 2.0-AIFunc，一个包含465个验证实例的基准，涵盖125个真实世界数据库，涉及Snowflake平台上的六种AI函数。我们从现有的企业文本到SQL基准出发，通过基于Agent的流水线构建Spider 2.0-AIFunc，将源任务重写为AI原生形式，同时转换目标查询并细化自然语言指令，使预期的AI原生解决方案明确并减少歧义。所有实例在发布前都经过跨时间窗口的多轮重复执行协议，以确认结果稳定性。评估了十个最先进的语言模型后，我们发现最强的专有模型达到67-70%的执行准确率，而最佳开源模型达到58.1%，这一差距主要源于谓词规范、模式基础和AI函数参数化方面的错误。为传统文本到SQL挑战设计的Agent框架（如模式检索和相关表选择）不能有效迁移到AI原生SQL：一个最小的Agent设置始终匹配或超过更复杂的替代方案，表明这些框架采用的策略在此设置中不那么关键。数据可在https://github.com/Leolty/Spider2-AIFunc获取。

Original abstract: Major cloud data platforms now expose large language model capabilities as native SQL functions, enabling analysts to perform classification, filtering, sentiment analysis, extraction, similarity search, and aggregation within ordinary SQL queries. Yet existing text-to-SQL benchmarks evaluate only conventional SQL and provide no signal on whether models can generate such AI-native SQL. We introduce Spider 2.0-AIFunc, a benchmark of 465 verified instances across 125 real-world databases covering six types of AI functions on the Snowflake platform. Starting from an existing enterprise text-to-SQL benchmark, we construct Spider 2.0-AIFunc through an agent-based pipeline that rewrites source tasks into AI-native form, simultaneously transforming target queries and refining natural language instructions to make the intended AI-native solution explicit and reduce ambiguity. All instances pass a multi-round repeated execution protocol across temporally separated windows to confirm result stability before release. Evaluating ten state-of-the-art language models, we find that the strongest proprietary models reach 67-70% execution accuracy while the best open-source model achieves 58.1%, a gap driven primarily by errors in predicate specification, schema grounding, and AI function parameterization. Agent frameworks designed for traditional text-to-SQL challenges, such as schema retrieval and relevant table selection, do not transfer effectively to AI-native SQL: a minimal agent setup consistently matches or outperforms more elaborate alternatives, suggesting that the strategies these frameworks employ are less critical in this setting. Data are available at https://github.com/Leolty/Spider2-AIFunc .

</details>


### [73] [From Voting to Agent Collaboration: Answer-Type-Aware LLM Pipelines for BioASQ 14b](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06452v1)
*Taeyun Roh,Eunha Lee,Wonjune Jang,Sohyun Chung,Junha Jung,Jaewoo Kang*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 问题类型感知的多agent流水线用于QA，多agent协作方法有迁移价值。

TL;DR: 提出了一种针对问题类型的LLM框架，在BioASQ 14b中通过不同策略处理是/否、事实和列表问题，并在事实子任务中获得第一名。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 生物医学问答需要准确提取和跨文档整合证据，但传统单一提示策略无法适应不同问题类型的推理需求。

Method: 根据问题类型选择不同流程：是/否用片段洗牌和自反思；事实用完整片段和思维链上下文学习；列表用多智能体协作提取、生成、验证和聚合。

Result: 在BioASQ 14b官方评估中，框架在多个批次表现竞争性，并在第4批次事实子任务获第一名。

Conclusion: 结合问题类型特异性推理、集成预测和智能体验证可有效提升生物医学问答的可靠性。

中文摘要：生物医学问答不仅需要从科学文献中准确提取信息，还需要跨多个文档可靠地整合证据。本研究提出了一种针对问题类型的大语言模型（LLM）框架，用于BioASQ 14b Task B，旨在提高生物医学问答中答案的鲁棒性和证据基础。该框架不是对所有问题应用单一的提示策略，而是根据是/否、事实和列表问题各自不同的推理和评估要求，选择不同的推理流程。对于是/否问题，使用片段洗牌和自我反思来减少对证据顺序的敏感性并提高决策稳定性。对于事实问题，结合完整片段输入和基于思维链的上下文学习，以支持准确的生物医学实体识别。对于列表问题，采用多智能体架构，其中证据提取、候选生成、答案验证和最终聚合协同处理。在BioASQ 13b上的初步实验用于确定每种问题类型的有效推理策略，随后在官方BioASQ 14b Task B挑战中评估了该框架。在官方评估中，我们的框架在多个批次中表现出竞争力，并在第4批次的事实子任务中获得了第一名。这些结果证明了将针对问题类型的推理、集成预测和基于智能体的验证相结合，对于可靠的生物医学问答的有效性。

Original abstract: Biomedical question answering requires not only accurate extraction of information from scientific literature but also reliable integration of evidence across multiple documents. This study presents a question-type-specific large language model (LLM) framework for BioASQ 14b Task B, designed to improve answer robustness and evidence grounding in biomedical question answering. Rather than applying a single prompting strategy to all questions, the framework selects different inference procedures for yes/no, factoid, and list questions according to their distinct reasoning and evaluation requirements. For yes/no questions, snippet shuffling and self-reflection are used to reduce sensitivity to evidence ordering and improve decision stability. For factoid questions, full-snippet input is combined with chain-of-thought-based in-context learning to support accurate biomedical entity identification. For list questions, a multi-agent architecture is employed, in which evidence extraction, candidate generation, answer verification, and final aggregation are handled collaboratively. Preliminary experiments on BioASQ 13b were used to identify effective inference strategies for each question type, and the resulting framework was subsequently evaluated in the official BioASQ 14b Task B challenge. In the official evaluation, our framework showed competitive performance across multiple batches and achieved first place in the factoid subtask of Batch 4. These results demonstrate the effectiveness of combining question-type-specific inference, ensemble prediction, and agent-based verification for reliable biomedical question answering.

</details>

### [74] [The Balkanization of Execution-Security Research for AI Coding Agents: Isolation, Access Control, and Time-of-Check-to-Time-of-Use Vulnerabilities](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05743v1)
*Mohammadreza Rashidi*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: 系统化分析coding agent执行安全，直接相关agent安全控制。

TL;DR: 系统化39篇AI编码智能体执行安全论文（2023-2026），识别17个类别和5个交叉空白，提出研究议程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有AI编码智能体执行安全文献分散，缺乏系统化梳理，导致关键交叉空白未被识别。

Method: 对39篇论文进行系统化分类为17个类别，并通过验证协议确认4个CVE，跨类别分析识别5个空白。

Result: 识别出5个交叉空白：隔离架构缺乏统一基准评估、策略执行与隔离研究脱节、TOCTOU与MCP威胁未统一分析、忽略策略编写错误、未处理良性越界动作。

Conclusion: 本文填补了执行安全系统化空白，并提出针对5个空白的研究议程。

中文摘要：AI编码智能体现在能够读取仓库、调用工具并执行shell命令，且人类监督有限。关于其执行层安全性的研究正在快速增长，但相关文献较为分散。关于沙箱隔离、能力与访问控制、策略执行、检查时间到使用时间（TOCTOU）竞争、模型上下文协议（MCP）威胁、身份委托、执行溯源、网络出口控制以及智能体生成代码的静态分析等论文，均独立发表且极少相互引用。我们将2023年至2026年间发表的39篇论文系统化为17个类别，每个类别均直接对照原始来源进行验证。相同的验证协议还确认了四个直接影响生产环境智能体框架的已披露并修复的CVE。跨类别阅读揭示了五个没有单篇论文涉及到的交叉性空白。（1）隔离架构和能力模型几乎从未在共享基准上相互评估。（2）策略执行研究报告的真实拒绝列表失败率从69%到98%，但没有任何隔离论文在该对抗设置下重新评估自身防御。（3）TOCTOU和MCP威胁被作为独立文献分析，尽管两者都是同一状态验证问题的实例。（4）每种执行机制都假设策略编写者诚实，从而忽略了策略编写错误本身。（5）在现实提示下，良性但超出范围的智能体动作发生率高达17.1%，而该语料库中没有任何访问控制或能力论文对此加以处理。现有的智能体AI安全更广泛综述仅将沙箱作为众多防御中的一项加以讨论，导致执行安全缺乏专门的系统化。本文旨在填补这一空白。最后，我们针对这五个空白提出了研究议程。

Original abstract: AI coding agents now read repositories, call tools, and execute shell commands with limited human oversight, and a fast-growing body of work studies whether the execution layer around them is actually safe. That literature is scattered. Papers on sandbox isolation, capability and access control, policy enforcement, time-of-check-to-time-of-use (TOCTOU) races, Model Context Protocol (MCP) threats, identity delegation, execution provenance, network egress control, and static analysis of agent-generated code are published independently and rarely cite one another. We systematize 39 papers published between 2023 and 2026 into 17 categories, each verified directly against its source. The same verification protocol also confirms four disclosed, patched CVEs directly affecting production agent harnesses. Reading across categories surfaces five cross-cutting gaps that no single paper addresses. (1) Isolation architectures and capability models are almost never evaluated against one another on a shared benchmark. (2) Policy-enforcement studies report failure rates from 69% to 98% of real denylists, yet no isolation paper re-evaluates its own defense under that adversarial setting. (3) TOCTOU and MCP threats are analyzed as separate literatures despite both being instances of the same state-validation problem. (4) Every enforcement mechanism assumes an honest policy author, leaving policy-authoring error itself unaddressed. (5) Benign but out-of-scope agent actions occurring at rates up to 17.1% under realistic prompting are addressed by no access-control or capability paper in the corpus. Existing broader surveys of agentic AI security discuss sandboxing only as one item among many defenses, leaving execution security without a dedicated systematization. This paper is written to fill that gap. We conclude with a research agenda directed at the five gaps.

</details>


### [75] [Unicode TAG-Block Concealment of Tool-Metadata Payloads in the Model Context Protocol: An Approval-View Fidelity Gap Across Three Independent Server Implementations](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05744v1)
*Mohammadreza Rashidi*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: MCP协议存在隐藏编码漏洞，使攻击者可通过Unicode TAG块向模型注入恶意负载，绕过人类审查。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 编码代理通过MCP协议调用外部工具时，人类审查与模型实际接收内容不一致，存在安全漏洞。

Method: 通过分析协议间隙，发现Unicode TAG块编码可隐藏有效负载；构建概念验证攻击，测试5个元数据表面、8种技术，并跨3个服务器库验证。

Result: 8/8技术成功注入负载，4/8规避清理器，TAG块编码完全隐藏；协议强制重新批准率为0。

Conclusion: MCP协议设计存在根本性安全缺陷，需重新设计元数据处理方式以确保人类审查的可靠性。

中文摘要：模型上下文协议（MCP）是编码代理发现和调用外部工具的主要方式。服务器通过tools/list握手通告每个工具，返回名称、自然语言描述和JSON输入模式。客户端在一次性批准对话框中渲染此元数据，然后在后续每一轮中逐字注入到模型上下文中。协议中没有任何要求渲染的批准视图和传递给模型的字节匹配。我们将这一差距孤立为单一结构机制——隐藏编码，并通过无模型、无协议的分析表明，Unicode的TAG块（U+E0000到U+E007F）在任何主流终端、聊天或IDE渲染器中都没有分配字形，因此用其编写的有效负载在人类审查者看来是缺失的，同时逐字节地存活到模型的标记器中。然后，我们测量这种机制是否真的击败了当今的客户端防御，构建了一个概念验证，该验证针对真实的客户端和服务器使用真实的MCP JSON-RPC/stdio协议。在5个不同的MCP元数据表面上，我们使用确定性的协议级工具实现了8种具体技术。所有8/8的技术都将攻击者控制的有效负载传递到模型上下文中，4/8规避了代表性的字符串匹配清理器，并且正如机制分析所预测的那样，只有TAG块编码（1/8）在人类批准视图中不可见，同时仍然逐字到达模型。MCP强制重新批准0/8的技术，即使在检查时间到使用时间的抽地毯攻击下也是如此。为了测试这些结果是协议的特性还是一个服务器代码库的工件，我们针对3个独立开发的Python MCP服务器库重新实现了目录，发现所有32个跨库结果单元完全一致。基线清理器标记了25个良性描述中的0个。

Original abstract: The Model Context Protocol (MCP) is the dominant way coding agents discover and invoke external tools. A server advertises each tool through a tools/list handshake that returns a name, a natural-language description, and a JSON input schema. The client renders this metadata once, in a one-time approval dialog, and then injects it verbatim into the model's context on every subsequent turn. Nothing in the protocol requires the rendered approval view and the bytes delivered to the model to match. We isolate that gap as a single structural mechanism, concealment encoding, and show with a model-free, protocol-free analysis that Unicode's TAG block (U+E0000 to U+E007F) has no assigned glyph in any mainstream terminal, chat, or IDE renderer, so a payload written in it is absent from what a human reviewer sees while surviving byte-for-byte into the model's tokenizer. We then measure whether this mechanism actually defeats today's client-side defenses, building a proof-of-concept that speaks the real MCP JSON-RPC/stdio protocol against a genuine client and server. Across 5 distinct MCP metadata surfaces we implement 8 concrete techniques with a deterministic, protocol-level harness. All 8/8 techniques deliver an attacker-controlled payload into the model's context, 4/8 evade a representative string-matching sanitizer, and exactly as the mechanism analysis predicts, only the TAG-block encoding (1/8) is invisible in the human approval view while still reaching the model verbatim. MCP forces re-approval for 0/8 techniques even under a time-of-check to time-of-use rug-pull. To test whether these outcomes are a property of the protocol or an artifact of one server codebase, we re-implement the catalogue against 3 independently developed Python MCP server libraries and find total agreement across all 32 cross-library outcome cells. The baseline sanitizer flags 0 of 25 benign descriptions.

</details>

### [78] [Multi-Channel Spread-Spectrum Code Watermarking](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06009v1)
*Soohyeon Choi,Debin Gao,Yue Duan*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出多通道扩频水印，首个24位有效载荷、无需训练、事后代码水印，具有形式化鲁棒性保证，在多种攻击下保持高准确率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有水印方案要么需要访问生成模型（无法用于第三方代码），要么有效载荷太小（最多4位）无法区分众多模型配置，且缺乏鲁棒性保证。

Method: 在变量命名约定和八对语义等价代码模式中编码比特，使用密钥伪随机排列将每个站点映射到码字比特，通过多数投票和里德-所罗门码实现鲁棒性。

Result: 在1,750个Python文件上实现100%干净检测准确率、零误报；在17种攻击下，8个变量重命名时准确率97.6%，10%随机破坏时94.1%，而基线在单变换下降至0%；嵌入和检测总计<200ms/CPU。

Conclusion: 多通道扩频水印是第一个满足代码归因需求的事后方案，兼具高有效载荷、强鲁棒性和高效性，可部署于实际场景。

中文摘要：将代码归因于生成它的大语言模型对于来源、许可和滥用问责至关重要，但目前尚无部署的水印满足这一需求。生成时方案需要访问生成模型，无法应用于第三方代码，而事后方案适用于任何代码但最多携带4位有效载荷，远不足以区分众多已部署的模型配置。我们提出了多通道扩频水印，这是第一个具有24位有效载荷和正式鲁棒性保证的事后、无需训练的代码水印。该方案在变量命名约定和八对语义等价的代码模式中编码比特，并通过密钥伪随机排列将每个站点映射到一个码字比特，使得每个比特获得多个独立投票。多数投票吸收分布式破坏，而外部里德-所罗门码在集中信道攻击击败投票时恢复标识符，从而为格式化、句法和结构攻击提供可证明的鲁棒性界限。在来自CodeNet以及GPT-4.1和Llama-4生成的1,750个Python文件上，该水印实现了100%的干净检测准确率和零误报。在17种攻击类型下，它在8个变量重命名下以97.6%的准确率恢复标识符，在10%随机逐位破坏下以94.1%的准确率恢复标识符，而最强的事后基线在任何单变换攻击下都降至0%。嵌入和检测合计在CPU上耗时不到200毫秒，无需训练数据或GPU。

Original abstract: Attributing code to the large language model that produced it is essential for provenance, licensing, and misuse accountability, yet no deployed watermark meets this need. Generation-time schemes require access to the producing model and cannot be applied to third-party code, while post-hoc schemes work on any code but carry at most 4 bits of payload, far too few to distinguish the many deployed model configurations. We present multi-channel spread-spectrum watermarking, the first post-hoc, training-free code watermark with a 24-bit payload and formal robustness guarantees. The scheme encodes bits in variable naming conventions and in eight pairs of semantically equivalent code patterns, and a keyed pseudo-random permutation maps every site to a codeword bit so that each bit receives multiple independent votes. Majority voting absorbs distributed corruption, while an outer Reed-Solomon code recovers the identifier when concentrated channel attacks defeat the vote, yielding provable robustness bounds for formatting, syntactic, and structural attacks. Across 1,750 Python files from CodeNet and from GPT-4.1 and Llama-4 generations, the watermark achieves 100% clean-detection accuracy with zero false positives. Under 17 attack types, it recovers the identifier at 97.6% accuracy under 8 variable renames and 94.1% under 10% random per-site corruption, while the strongest post-hoc baseline collapses to 0% under any single-transform attack. Embedding and detection together take under 200 ms on CPU without training data or GPU.

### [79] [Claimed or Attested? A Commit-Signature Dataset and Identity Trust Tiers across the World of Code](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06194v1)
*Audris Mockus*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: Summary generation failed


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Motivation analysis unavailable

Method: Method extraction failed

Result: Result analysis unavailable

Conclusion: Conclusion extraction failed

中文摘要：Abstract translation failed

Original abstract: An author string in a git commit is free text the committer typed, so identity resolution over a global commit corpus rests on a claim that nothing in the commit verifies. A cryptographically signed commit is different: it binds the commit to a key the committer controls, and when that key ties back to a real-world identity the git identity becomes attested rather than merely claimed. We release the first commit-signature axis for the World of Code (WoC), extracted for the V2604 collection. The signature travels in the commit object's gpgsig header and is already carried, unparsed, in the commit-message field of the WoC commit tables, so the axis is a scan over existing tables rather than a re-read of the object database. Over the V2604 corpus of 5,866,595,698 commits, 17.59% carry a signature (PGP dominant at 98.96%, with a growing minority of SSH and X.509/sigstore signatures), or 1,031,721,316 signed commits. We release the per-commit signature map c2sigFull, a key-to-author graph gated so that shared organization and continuous-integration keys are separated from person keys, and A2trust, a per-identity attestation tier (unsigned, signed, real-world-bound, cross-corpus attested) that extends the published A2cls identity-class dataset. The signature axis is a precision anchor, not a coverage layer: signed commits skew toward recent and security-conscious developers, a population that overlaps the scholarly authors a bibliography join targets. We use the person keys to build a cryptographically grounded alias gold that calibrates the heuristic WoC alias map independently of hand-labeled pairs, and to attach an attestation provenance to science-to-software identity links. All artifacts are released as a self-contained, in dependently hosted replication package keyed to the WoC V2604 collection.

### [80] [When Agents Go Rogue: Activation-Based Detection of Malicious Behaviors in Multi-Agent Systems](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06807v1)
*Haowen Xu,Xue Tan,Lei Ma,Zhihao Zhang,Chao Wang,Qingze Wang,Ping Chen,Jun Dai,Xiaoyan Sun*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: 多Agent系统恶意行为检测方法，对agent安全控制有启发。

TL;DR: AcMAS是一种基于激活空间分析的MAS恶意行为检测框架，无需显式交互图，能有效检测语义隐蔽攻击并恢复受损智能体，在同步和异步场景中均显著优于基线方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有MAS安全防御依赖显式恶意攻击假设和基于图的同步传播模型，无法应对语义隐蔽和异步执行的实际攻击。

Method: 提出AcMAS框架，通过分析本地智能体内部推理状态的激活空间来检测恶意行为，不依赖显式交互图，并基于激活分析信号恢复受损智能体功能。

Result: 在同步和异步设置中，AcMAS分别达到0.94和0.93的F1分数，相比图基线分别提升0.22和0.55，且能泛化到不同LLM骨干、攻击强度和系统规模。

Conclusion: AcMAS无需图建模即可鲁棒检测隐蔽攻击并修复受损智能体，为MAS安全提供了有效方案。

中文摘要：虽然基于LLM的多智能体系统（MAS）能够有效协作完成复杂任务，但由于智能体和交互层面的漏洞，它们面临严重的安全挑战。现有大多数MAS安全防御建立在两个核心假设之上：语义明确的恶意攻击以及基于显式图对MAS拓扑和智能体层面交互的建模。实际上，现实世界中的攻击变得更加语义隐蔽，同时MAS执行通常是异步的，不具备图传播模型所假设的时间对齐性。为解决这些限制，我们提出了AcMAS，一种基于激活的MAS恶意行为检测框架。通过分析本地智能体激活空间中的内部推理状态，AcMAS能够以同步鲁棒的方式检测即使隐蔽的攻击，无需依赖显式交互图。此外，我们的激活分析提供了关键信号，指导AcMAS恢复受损智能体的功能，而非如现有最优方法那样采用破坏性的隔离。全面评估表明，AcMAS在对抗隐蔽攻击方面显著优于基于图的基线，在同步设置中F1值提升+0.22（0.94 vs. 0.72），在异步设置中提升+0.55（0.93 vs. 0.38），并能在多种开源LLM骨干、攻击强度和MAS规模下泛化。

Original abstract: While enabling effective collaboration on complex tasks, LLM-based Multi-Agent Systems (MAS) face critical security challenges due to vulnerabilities at the agent and interaction levels. Most existing MAS security defenses are built upon two core assumptions: semantically-explicit malicious attacks and explicit graph-based modeling of the MAS topology and agent-level interactions. In practice, real-world attacks are becoming more semantically stealthy, while MAS execution is typically asynchronous without the temporal alignment assumed by graph-based propagation models. To address these limitations, we propose AcMAS, an activation-based framework for malicious-behavior detection in MAS. By analyzing internal reasoning states in the activation space of local agents, AcMAS detects even stealthy attacks in a synchronization-robust fashion, without relying on explicit interaction graphs. Moreover, our activation analysis provides critical signals to guide AcMAS in restoring the functionality of compromised agents, rather than the disruptive agent isolation commonly used by the state-of-the-art methods. Comprehensive evaluation demonstrates that AcMAS significantly outperforms graph-based baselines against stealthy attacks, by +0.22 F1 in synchronous settings (0.94 vs. 0.72) and by +0.55 F1 in asynchronous settings (0.93 vs. 0.38), with generalization across diverse open-source LLM backbones, attack intensity, and MAS scale.

</details>

TL;DR: 提出一个框架系统评估LLM编码代理的模型发现过程，量化变异性和影响因素，并通过实验验证了推理努力与成本、复杂性的关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM编码代理的随机性和适应性使其模型发现行为无法通过单一基准充分表征，需要系统性评估方法。

Method: 将代理视为随机模型发现算子，设计受控实验（推理努力、任务、指标、数据组成），进行回归分析和典型分解。

Result: 揭示了推理努力对输出质量、成本、时间和过程复杂性的影响，并发现推理努力的主导方向与性能-成本效用方向一致。

Conclusion: 该框架能有效评估LLM代理的模型发现行为，为理解其变异性提供了方法，并有助于优化代理使用策略。

中文摘要：大语言模型编码代理越来越多地执行开放式数据建模和分析。这些代理是随机且自适应的，因此它们的自主模型发现行为无法通过单个基准测试得到充分表征。在这项工作中，我们提出了一种实验设计和分析框架，用于系统评估这一发现过程，量化其变异性，并识别重要因素。所提出的框架将这些代理视为随机的模型发现算子，将特定任务的发现数据和优化目标映射到拟合模型。具体而言，我们在受控的实验因素下（包括代理的推理努力、任务、优化指标和训练数据组成）研究了两个这样的算子：Codex 和 Claude Code。对于每个代理-任务-指标组合，我们对多个响应变量（如输出质量、美元成本、挂钟时间和过程复杂性）进行回归模型和推断。此外，我们开发了一种与效用对齐的典型分解，以表征推理努力效应的主导方向，并评估该方向是否与性能-成本效用方向一致。所提出的框架在一个由网络化构词游戏构成的测试平台上进行了演示，并给出了关于推理努力与成本和过程复杂性的深刻发现。

Original abstract: Large language model coding agents increasingly perform open-ended data modeling and analysis. These agents are stochastic and adaptive, and therefore their autonomous model discovery behavior cannot be adequately characterized by a single benchmark run. In this work, we propose an experimental design and analysis framework for systematically evaluating this discovery process, quantifying its variability, and identifying important factors. The proposed framework treats these agents as stochastic model-discovery operators, which map task-specific discovery data and an optimization target to a fitted model. Specifically, we investigate two such operators, Codex and Claude Code, under controlled experimental factors including agent's reasoning effort, task, optimization metric, and composition of training data. For each agent-task-metric combination, regression models and inference are conducted for multiple responses such as output quality, dollar cost, wall-clock time, and process complexity. Furthermore, we develop a utility-aligned canonical decomposition to characterize the dominant direction of the reasoning-effort effect and to assess whether that direction aligns with a performance-cost utility direction. The proposed framework is demonstrated on a testbed of networked word-forming games with insightful findings on reasoning effort with respect to cost and process complexity.

</details>

### [84] [From Agentic to Autogenic Network Management for AI-Native 6G and Beyond: A Standards Perspective](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06786v1)
*Petar Djukic,Sudipta Acharya,Takai Eddine Kennouche,Burak Kantarci*

Main category: cs.NI

Selection reason: 提出自编程、自反思等agent能力，但领域特定于网络管理，对agent设计有潜在启发。

TL;DR: 提出一种自主网络管理参考架构，通过自我编程等能力扩展代理，支持分阶段部署，并基于运营商场景验证，最后给出研究路线图。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有网络管理方法在6G网络的规模和复杂性下难以实现基于Agentic AI的自主管理，需要能够自我生成和演进自动化软件的系统。

Method: 提出自主网络管理参考架构，增强代理的自我编程、自我反思、自我导向和自我架构能力，支持从人工监督到自主的分阶段部署。

Result: 通过TM Forum的高优先级运营商场景展示了该方法如何解决实际运营挑战。

Conclusion: 要实现6G中的自主网络管理，仍需进一步发展技术，并给出了研究路线图。

中文摘要：包括TM Forum、3GPP和ETSI在内的标准机构正趋同于将Agentic AI作为下一代网络管理的基础，其中基于大型AI模型（LAM）的代理能够自主解读意图、协调资源并在运行时调整运营行为。然而，要在6G网络的规模和复杂性下实现这一愿景，需要管理系统能够在运行过程中生成和演进自己的自动化软件。我们引入了自主网络管理（Autogenic network management），这是一种参考架构，将代理能力扩展为具备自我编程、自我反思、自我导向和自我架构的能力。该架构支持实用的分阶段部署，从人工监督的基于LAM的代理开始，随着信心的建立逐步向自主运营过渡。我们通过从TM Forum自治网络用例中提取的高优先级运营商场景来演示该方法，展示了自主管理如何解决实际的运营挑战。最后，我们提出了一份研究路线图，概述了使自主网络管理在未来6G网络中成为现实所需的技术进展。

Original abstract: Standards bodies, including TM Forum, 3GPP, and ETSI, are converging on Agentic AI as the foundation for next-generation network management, where Large AI Model (LAM)-based agents autonomously interpret intent, coordinate resources, and adapt operational behaviors at runtime. However, achieving this vision at the scale and complexity of 6G networks requires management systems that can generate and evolve their own automation software during operation. We introduce Autogenic network management, a reference architecture that extends agentic capabilities with self-programming, self reflection, self-orienting, and self-architecting capabilities. The architecture supports practical staged deployment beginning with human-supervised LAM-based agents and progressing toward autonomous operation as confidence builds. We demonstrate the approach through high-priority operator scenarios drawn from TM Forum's autonomous network use cases, showing how autogenic management addresses real operational challenges. We conclude with a research roadmap outlining the technical advances needed to make autogenic network management realistic in future 6G networks.

</details>

### [85] [What Predicts Correctness in Text-to-SQL? A Selective-Prediction Study](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06799v1)
*Robert Richardson*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 研究Text-to-SQL正确性预测，涉及验证器、置信度和选择性预测，对coding agent可靠性有参考。

TL;DR: AI生成的SQL查询正确性评估中，基于验证的信号（如LLM评判员）优于自一致性等黑盒信号，多提供商集成达到0.82 AUROC；微调验证器在领域内有效但跨模式泛化差，大型冻结推理模型更可靠。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 评估AI生成SQL查询的不确定性，需要识别能够正确预测查询是否与人工参考结果匹配的信号，以提高安全性和可靠性。

Method: 使用AUROC比较多种信号（自一致性、可执行性、LLM评判等）在BIRD和Spider基准上的预测效果，并测试双提供商集成以及微调验证器（编码器和生成式）的跨模式泛化能力。

Result: 最佳信号为LLM评判员集成（0.82 AUROC），自一致性最高0.675；微调验证器在分布内0.77-0.79，跨模式降至0.66，扩展模型和增加数据多样性未能改善。

Conclusion: 文本到SQL的正确性不确定性依赖于推理型信号，验证器在模式外泛化需大型冻结推理模型，而非微调模型。

中文摘要：评估AI生成的SQL查询中的不确定性需要估计查询是否正确，其中正确意味着它执行到与人工编写的参考相同的结果。我们研究了哪些信号能够在困难的表多文本到SQL任务上预测正确性，使用AUROC衡量每个信号将正确查询排在错误查询之上的效果。在BIRD和Spider上，黑盒信号如字符串、结构和执行自一致性、模式相关性分数以及查询可执行性均在约0.61到0.68 AUROC之间，其中字符串自一致性最强（0.675）；白盒对数概率类似（0.67）。超越这一上限的信号是基于验证的：LLM评判员得分从0.72（GPT-4o-mini）到0.78（Claude）。来自不同提供商的评判员会犯不同的错误，因此一个双提供商集成达到了0.82 AUROC，具有良好校准的概率（期望校准误差0.03），并支持有用的弃权边界（例如，在24%的选择性风险下回答27%的问题），而自一致性没有提供有效的低风险子集。该模式在两个基准、两个生成器和两个评判员提供商上一致。我们还询问是否能够训练一个验证器。微调后的验证器，无论是编码器还是生成式，在分布内达到约0.77到0.79 AUROC，但在未见模式上下降到约0.66；扩展到7B、增加模式多样性、蒸馏强评判员的推理以及跨基准训练均未能缩小这一差距。跨模式迁移似乎追踪模型规模和推理而非微调。在实践中，文本到SQL的正确性不确定性存在于基于推理的信号中：微调验证器是一个良好的领域内工具，但能够在模式间泛化的验证器目前意味着一个大型冻结推理模型。

Original abstract: Evaluating uncertainty in AI-generated SQL queries requires estimating whether a query is correct, where correct means it executes to the same result as a human-written reference. We study which signals predict correctness on hard multi-table text-to-SQL, using AUROC to measure how well each ranks correct queries above incorrect ones. On BIRD and Spider, black-box signals such as string, structural, and execution self-consistency, a schema-relevance score, and query executability all fall between about 0.61 and 0.68 AUROC, with string self-consistency strongest at 0.675; white-box log-probability is similar (0.67). The signals that move past this ceiling are verification-based: an LLM judge scores from 0.72 (GPT-4o-mini) to 0.78 (Claude). Judges from different providers make different errors, so a two-provider ensemble reaches 0.82 AUROC with a well-calibrated probability (expected calibration error 0.03) and supports useful abstention frontiers (for example, answering 27% of questions at 24% selective risk) where self-consistency offers no valid low-risk subset. The pattern holds across two benchmarks, two generators, and two judge providers. We also ask whether a verifier can be trained. Fine-tuned verifiers, both encoder and generative, reach about 0.77 to 0.79 AUROC in-distribution but fall to about 0.66 on unseen schemas; scaling to 7B, adding schema diversity, distilling a strong judge's rationales, and cross-benchmark training all fail to close that gap. Cross-schema transfer appears to track model scale and reasoning rather than fine-tuning. In practice, correctness uncertainty for text-to-SQL lives in reasoning-based signals: a fine-tuned verifier is a good in-domain tool, but a verifier that generalizes across schemas currently means a large frozen reasoning model.

</details>


### [86] [A Gold-Standard Study of What Makes a Lightweight Game-Playing Agent Strong](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06854v1)
*Nima Kelidari,Mohammadsaeed Haghi,Mahdi Salmani*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 游戏agent训练策略研究，涉及信任区域、课程学习等，对agent训练有参考。

TL;DR: 通过信任域更新、奖励设计、课程学习等技巧，将自对弈智能体对抗规则专家的胜率从30%提升至36%，但网络容量并非瓶颈，最终给出一种轻量级通用训练方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 不完美信息卡牌游戏中，强化学习智能体受限于训练对手强度，且难以评估性能（因随机对手太弱、自对弈又无法区分强弱）。因此需要一个强基准专家作为标尺，并系统研究哪些设计选择能提升轻量级智能体的能力。

Method: 构建固定规则专家仅用于评估；在超百次运行中隔离出有效技巧（信任域更新、奖励设计、课程学习、热启动、保留最佳检查点）；比较多种编码器；添加标准基线（神经虚拟自对弈和信息集蒙特卡洛搜索）；在勒杜克德州扑克上验证可迁移性。

Result: 专家击败所有训练智能体70-99%概率；叠加最佳技巧使自对弈冠军胜率从30%升至36%；奖励塑造、学习状态嵌入、模仿学习、LLM对手等无效；网络容量增加未突破性能上限。

Conclusion: 提出一种轻量级、游戏无关的配方，无需使用专家进行训练即可获得有竞争力的智能体，适用于小模型可处理的任何游戏，并以稳健统计报告和可复用包形式发布。

中文摘要：强化学习智能体在不完美信息卡牌游戏中的能力取决于其训练的对手，且难以评估，因为智能体击败随机对手的概率超过99%，而与自身副本对局则只能打成平手。为此，我们为金拉米构建了一个强大且固定的规则专家，仅将其作为评估基准，而非用于训练。该专家能以70%至99%的概率击败我们训练的所有智能体。在超过一百次运行中，我们揭示了哪些因素能增强轻量级智能体的实力：信任域更新、精准设计的奖励、难度递增的对手课程、热启动以及保留最佳检查点均有帮助，将这些技巧叠加后，自对弈冠军对抗专家的胜率从约30%提升至36%。有些想法并未奏效：短期与长期奖励塑造、学习状态嵌入、模仿学习与DAgger、以及实时大型语言模型对手要么无益，要么过慢，要么难以大规模训练。对比MLP、卷积、集合、注意力及循环编码器后发现，增加容量几乎无法突破上限，这表明瓶颈在于信息而非网络规模。我们加入标准基线方法（神经虚拟自对弈和信息集蒙特卡洛搜索），并确认该方法可迁移至勒杜克德州扑克（其最优解可计算）。最终我们得到一种轻量级、游戏无关的配方，无需专家参与训练即可训练出有竞争力的智能体，适用于任何小型模型能够处理的游戏，并以稳健的统计报告呈现，同时以可复用包的形式发布。

Original abstract: Reinforcement learning agents for imperfect-information card games are only as strong as the opponents they train against, and they are hard to grade, since they beat a random opponent over 99 percent of the time and only tie copies of themselves. So we build a strong, fixed, rule-based expert for Gin Rummy and use it only as a yardstick, never for training. It beats every agent we trained 70 to 99 percent of the time. Across more than a hundred runs, we isolate what makes a lightweight agent stronger. Trust region updates, a well-aimed reward, a curriculum of tougher opponents, warm starting, and keeping the best checkpoint all help, and stacking them lifts a self-play champion from about 30 to 36 percent against the expert. Several ideas did not pay off. Short-term and longer-term reward shaping, learned state embeddings, imitation and DAgger, and a live large language model opponent were each unhelpful, too slow, or too heavy to train at scale. Comparing MLP, convolutional, set-based, attention, and recurrent encoders shows that extra capacity does little to break the ceiling, suggesting the limit is information rather than network size. We add standard baselines (neural fictitious self-play and information set Monte Carlo search) and confirm the approach carries over to Leduc Hold'em, where the optimum is computable. The result is a lightweight, game-agnostic recipe that trains competitive agents without training on the expert, for any game a small model can handle, reported with robust statistics and released as a reusable package.

</details>

### [87] [Harnessing Code Agents for Automatic Software Verification](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06341v1)
*Shuangxiang Kan,Shuanglong Kan,Sebastian Ertel*

Main category: cs.FL

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 通过将整个引理交给LLM代码智能体并封装在验证框架中，实现了对所有目标引理的完全自动证明，无需专家干预。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有形式化验证方法需要大量专家努力，LLM生成证明的方法受限于固定策略，只能证明一小部分定理。

Method: 将整个引理交给通用的LLM代码智能体（如Claude Code），让其自由选择方法，并封装在验证框架中提供反馈和硬约束，确保证明的可靠性、完整性和终止性。

Result: 在Iris上证明了所有4257个引理和Rust标准库的217个引理；在reglang上证明了全部318个引理（此前仅1/8）；在iris-lean上证明了72个未移植引理。

Conclusion: 该方法证明了强加固定策略是不必要的，通用LLM代码智能体结合验证框架可以完全自动地实现形式化验证。

中文摘要：形式化验证提供了软件正确性的最强保证，但它无法扩展：交互式定理证明器（如 Coq）所需的证明需要巨大的专家努力。大型语言模型有望自动生成这些证明，然而现有方法将固定的人工设计的证明策略嵌入系统，并约束模型遵循该策略（逐步检索前提和预测策略，或通过分治策略拆分目标），但仍只能证明目标定理的一小部分。我们表明，强加这样的策略是不必要且具有局限性的。将整个引理交给一个通用的大型语言模型代码智能体（例如 Claude Code），让其自由选择自己的方法，并将其封装在验证框架中，既更简单又更有效，实现了完全覆盖：每个目标引理都被证明，没有失败，也不需要 Coq 专家干预。该智能体在框架的反馈和硬约束下编写证明，这些约束确保每个证明是可靠的（仅当证明器的内核关闭时才被接受）、完整的（没有未证明或被静默丢弃的义务）和终止的（没有发散的策略）。我们从三个维度评估了这个框架加代码智能体。（1）核心逻辑：在 Iris（一种用于并发和内存操作程序的最先进的分离逻辑）上，Aria 完全自动地证明了四个核心模块的全部 4,257 个引理以及基于它构建的 Rust 标准库的 217 个引理。（2）与先前 LLM 证明器的比较：在 reglang 上，先前证明器勉强能证明八分之一，而 Aria 证明了全部 318 个。（3）通用性：在 iris-lean（Iris 未完成的 Lean 4 移植版）上，它证明了 72 个尚未移植的引理，表明该方法并非特定于 Coq。最先进的模型（Claude Opus 4.7）可以完全自动地为验证过的软件开发编写证明。

Original abstract: Formal verification offers the strongest guarantee of software correctness, but it does not scale: the proofs demanded by interactive theorem provers such as Coq require enormous expert effort. Large language models (LLMs) promise to generate these proofs automatically, yet existing approaches wire a fixed, human-designed proof strategy into the system and constrain the model to follow it (retrieving premises and predicting tactics one step at a time, or splitting goals by divide-and-conquer), and still prove only a fraction of their target theorems.
  We show that imposing such a strategy is unnecessary and limiting. Handing the whole lemma to a general LLM code agent (for example, Claude Code), free to choose its own approach, and wrapping it in a verification harness is both simpler and more effective, achieving full coverage: every targeted lemma proved, with no failures and no Coq expert intervention. The agent writes the proofs under feedback and hard constraints from the harness that keep each one sound (accepted only when the prover's kernel closes it), complete (no obligation left unproved or silently dropped), and terminating (no divergent tactics).
  We evaluate this harness plus code agent along three dimensions. (1) Core logic: on Iris, the state-of-the-art separation logic for concurrent and memory-manipulating programs, Aria proves all 4,257 lemmas of the four core modules and the 217 lemmas verifying Rust's standard libraries built on it, fully automatically. (2) Comparison with prior LLM provers: on reglang, where prior provers manage barely one in eight, Aria proves all 318. (3) Generality: on iris-lean, the unfinished Lean 4 port of Iris, it proves 72 not-yet-ported lemmas, showing the approach is not specific to Coq. A state-of-the-art model (Claude Opus 4.7) can write proofs for verified software development fully and automatically.

</details>


<div id='cs.NE'></div>

# cs.NE [[Back]](#toc)

### [88] [Do You Remember? Toward Memory-Centric Multimodal AI](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11919v1)
*Xuguang Yu,Weigang Zheng,Minyue Yu*

Main category: cs.NE

Selection reason: 提出记忆中心架构，对agent记忆设计有参考。

TL;DR: 提出DoYouRemember架构，通过三阶段过程引入重构性记忆；发现LLM隐藏状态不含可恢复视觉信息，但共享记忆矩阵通过局部EMA更新可有效训练，其连续表示超越VQ基线，并统一解释了幻觉的必然性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 人类记忆是重构性的，而当前多模态大语言模型缺乏这种能力，它们处理图像后丢弃内部表示，无法记忆视觉信息。

Method: 三阶段架构：VQ-VAE压缩图像为离散视觉标记，LoRA微调的LLM联合注意视觉与文本标记，扩散解码器从LLM隐藏状态重建图像；训练共享记忆矩阵M时采用局部EMA更新（每个图像仅更新其64个槽中的前8个）以克服梯度抵消。

Result: LLM隐藏状态几乎不含可恢复视觉信息；M矩阵（229K参数，16倍压缩）在未见测试图像上接近VQ上限，扩展到1024槽时超越VQ（LPIPS 0.056 vs. 0.071），连续表示避免了量化误差。

Conclusion: 记忆是有损压缩，回忆是解压缩，幻觉是有损解压缩的内在属性而非缺陷。

中文摘要：人类的记忆是重构性的，而不是忠实的记录。当前的多模态大语言模型（MLLMs）缺乏这种能力：它们通过冻结的视觉编码器处理图像，产生一次性文本输出，并丢弃内部表示。我们提出了DoYouRemember，一种将重构性记忆引入MLLMs的三阶段架构：（1）VQ-VAE将图像压缩为离散的视觉标记，（2）LoRA微调的LLM联合关注视觉和文本标记，以及（3）扩散解码器从LLM的隐藏状态重建图像。在1,000张3D面部皮肤纹理图和99,000张无标签面部图像上，我们发现LLM隐藏状态包含约零可恢复的视觉信息——从VQ-VAE标记（LLM之前）生成清晰重建的同一解码器，从LLM隐藏状态（LLM之后）生成纯噪声，这表明LLM理解图像但不记忆它们。在反向传播下训练共享记忆矩阵M由于梯度抵消（O(1/sqrt(N))衰减）而系统性失败。我们确定了三个根本原因，并表明局部EMA更新解决了所有三个原因：每个图像仅更新其64个槽中的前8个，保持槽间多样性。得到的M（229K参数，压缩16倍）在未见测试图像上接近VQ上限。扩展到1,024个槽超过该上限（LPIPS 0.056 vs. 0.071），因为M的连续表示避免了VQ量化误差。我们在信息论框架下统一这些发现：记忆是有损压缩，回忆是解压缩，幻觉是有损解压缩的内在属性而非缺陷。

Original abstract: Human memory is reconstructive, not a faithful recording. Current multimodal LLMs (MLLMs) lack this capability: they process images through a frozen visual encoder, produce a one-shot text output, and discard internal representations. We present DoYouRemember, a three-stage architecture introducing reconstructive memory into MLLMs: (1) a VQ-VAE compresses images into discrete visual tokens, (2) a LoRA-fine-tuned LLM jointly attends to visual and text tokens, and (3) a Diffusion Decoder reconstructs images from the LLM's hidden states. On 1,000 3D facial skin texture maps and 99,000 unlabeled facial images, we find that LLM hidden states contain approximately zero recoverable visual information -- the same Decoder producing clear reconstructions from VQ-VAE tokens (pre-LLM) produces pure noise from LLM hidden states (post-LLM), demonstrating that the LLM understands images but does not remember them. Training a shared memory matrix M under backpropagation systematically fails due to gradient cancellation (O(1/sqrt(N)) attenuation). We identify three root causes and show that local EMA updating resolves all three: each image updates only its top-8 slots out of 64, preserving inter-slot diversity. The resulting M (229K parameters, 16x compressed) approaches the VQ upper bound on unseen test images. Scaling to 1,024 slots surpasses it (LPIPS 0.056 vs. 0.071), as M's continuous representation avoids VQ quantization error. We unify these findings under an information-theoretic framework: memory is lossy compression, recall is decompression, and hallucination is an inherent property of lossy decompression rather than a defect.

</details>
